FNV PPLIGHTING +0xDC FIELD WRITER PROVENANCE AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which constructors or init/copy functions reference the PPLighting-like vtable starts?
2. Do those same functions write, clear, copy, addref, or release field +0xDC?
3. Are broad renderer +0xDC writers actually tied to PPLighting shader-property classes?
4. If not, which exact provenance gap remains before Psycho can consume +0xDC for PBR?
